+        )

+00006980: 0a3c 6832 3e3c 6120 636c 6173 733d 2274  .<h2><a class="t
+00006990: 6f63 2d62 6163 6b72 6566 2220 6872 6566  oc-backref" href
+000069a0: 3d22 2374 6f63 2d65 6e74 7279 2d36 223e  ="#toc-entry-6">
+000069b0: 426f 6f73 7472 6170 204d 6f64 6966 6963  Boostrap Modific
+000069c0: 6174 696f 6e73 3a3c 2f61 3e3c 2f68 323e  ations:</a></h2>
+000069d0: 0a3c 703e 5468 6520 7072 6f64 7563 7420  .<p>The product 
+000069e0: 7069 636b 6572 2076 6965 7720 636f 6e74  picker view cont
+000069f0: 6169 6e65 7220 6861 7665 2061 2063 7573  ainer have a cus
+00006a00: 746f 6d20 6d65 6469 6120 7175 6572 6965  tom media querie
+00006a10: 7320 7370 6163 6520 6164 6469 6e67 2061  s space adding a
+00006a20: 206e 6577 2073 6372 6565 6e20 7369 7a65   new screen size
+00006a30: 2063 616c 6c65 6420 e280 9878 786c e280   called ...xxl..
+00006a40: 9920 2826 6774 3b3d 2031 3434 3070 7829  . (&gt;= 1440px)
+00006a50: 2061 6e64 206d 6f64 6966 6965 7320 7468   and modifies th
+00006a60: 6520 636f 6c75 6d6e 7320 746f 2068 6176  e columns to hav
+00006a70: 6520 3234 2069 6e73 7465 6164 206f 6620  e 24 instead of 
+00006a80: 3132 2e0a 5468 6973 206d 6561 6e73 2074  12..This means t
+00006a90: 6861 7420 796f 7520 6361 6e20 7573 6520  hat you can use 
+00006aa0: e280 9c63 6f6c 2d78 786c 2de2 809d 2069  ...col-xxl-... i
+00006ab0: 6e73 6964 6520 7468 6520 7072 6f64 7563  nside the produc
+00006ac0: 7420 7069 636b 6572 2076 6965 7720 636f  t picker view co
+00006ad0: 6e74 6169 6e65 722e 3c2f 703e 0a3c 2f64  ntainer.</p>.</d
+00006ae0: 6976 3e0a 3c2f 6469 763e 0a3c 6469 7620  iv>.</div>.<div 
+00006af0: 636c 6173 733d 2273 6563 7469 6f6e 2220  class="section" 
+00006b00: 6964 3d22 7573 6167 6522 3e0a 3c68 313e  id="usage">.<h1>
+00006b10: 3c61 2063 6c61 7373 3d22 746f 632d 6261  <a class="toc-ba
+00006b20: 636b 7265 6622 2068 7265 663d 2223 746f  ckref" href="#to
+00006b30: 632d 656e 7472 792d 3722 3e55 7361 6765  c-entry-7">Usage
+00006b40: 3c2f 613e 3c2f 6831 3e0a 3c70 3e57 6865  </a></h1>.<p>Whe
+00006b50: 6e20 796f 7520 6368 616e 6765 2074 6865  n you change the
+00006b60: 2076 616c 7565 206f 6620 6120 6669 656c   value of a fiel
+00006b70: 6420 616e 6420 7377 6974 6368 2074 6f20  d and switch to 
+00006b80: 6564 6974 2061 6e6f 7468 6572 2072 6563  edit another rec
+00006b90: 6f72 642c 2074 6865 0a63 6861 6e67 6573  ord, the.changes
+00006ba0: 2077 696c 6c20 6265 2061 7070 6c69 6564   will be applied
+00006bb0: 2074 6f20 7468 6520 7072 6576 696f 7573   to the previous
+00006bc0: 2072 6563 6f72 6420 7769 7468 6f75 7420   record without 
+00006bd0: 6861 7669 6e67 2074 6f20 636c 6963 6b20  having to click 
+00006be0: 6f6e 0a61 6363 6570 7420 6368 616e 6765  on.accept change
+00006bf0: 732e 3c2f 703e 0a3c 6469 7620 636c 6173  s.</p>.<div clas
+00006c00: 733d 2273 6563 7469 6f6e 2220 6964 3d22  s="section" id="
+00006c10: 7061 7274 732d 6f66 2d74 6865 2d77 6964  parts-of-the-wid
+00006c20: 6765 7422 3e0a 3c68 323e 3c61 2063 6c61  get">.<h2><a cla
+00006c30: 7373 3d22 746f 632d 6261 636b 7265 6622  ss="toc-backref"
+00006c40: 2068 7265 663d 2223 746f 632d 656e 7472   href="#toc-entr
+00006c50: 792d 3822 3e50 6172 7473 206f 6620 7468  y-8">Parts of th
+00006c60: 6520 7769 6467 6574 3a3c 2f61 3e3c 2f68  e widget:</a></h
+00006c70: 323e 0a3c 626c 6f63 6b71 756f 7465 3e0a  2>.<blockquote>.
